class="heading-col"><h3 class="heading">About <!-- -->Bitcoin</h3></div><div class="heading-col"><span class="title">Category</span><div class="title-icon"><div class="title-heading"><span>Currency</span><div class="__react_component_tooltip place-top type-dark" id="tooltip-sector" data-id="tooltip"></div><img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMTgiIGhlaWdodD0iMTgiIHhtbG5zPSJodHRwOi8vd3d3LnczLm9yZy8yMDAwL3N2ZyI+PGcgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSI+PGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iOCIgY3k9IjgiIHI9IjgiIHN0cm9rZT0iI0ZDQzExNyIgdHJhbnNmb3JtPSJ0cmFuc2xhdGUoMSAxKSIvPjxwYXRoIGQ9Ik0xMCA2VjRIOHYyaDJ6bTAgOFY3SDh2N2gyeiIgZmlsbD0iI0ZDQzExNyIvPjwvZz48L3N2Zz4=" data-for="tooltip-sector" data-tip="Intended to duplicate some or all of the functions of money" class="svg-icon"/></div></div></div><div class="heading-col"><span class="title">Value proposition</span><div class="title-icon"><div class="title-heading"><span>Digital gold</span><div class="__react_component_tooltip place-top type-dark" id="tooltip-proposition" data-id="tooltip"></div><img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMTgiIGhlaWdodD0iMTgiIHhtbG5zPSJodHRwOi8vd3d3LnczLm9yZy8yMDAwL3N2ZyI+PGcgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSI+PGNpcmNsZSBjeD0iOCIgY3k9IjgiIHI9IjgiIHN0cm9rZT0iI0ZDQzExNyIgdHJhbnNmb3JtPSJ0cmFuc2xhdGUoMSAxKSIvPjxwYXRoIGQ9Ik0xMCA2VjRIOHYyaDJ6bTAgOFY3SDh2N2gyeiIgZmlsbD0iI0ZDQzExNyIvPjwvZz48L3N2Zz4=" data-for="tooltip-proposition" data-tip="Attempts to duplicate gold&#x27;s bearer-instrument and scarcity qualities" class="svg-icon"/></div></div></div></div><div class="coin-about-text"><p><a href="/learn/bitcoin-101/what-is-bitcoin">Bitcoin</a> was the first cryptocurrency to successfully record transactions on a secure, decentralized <a href="/learn/blockchain-101/what-is-blockchain-technology">blockchain-based network</a>. Launched in early 2009 by its pseudonymous creator <a target="_blank" rel="noopener" href="/people/satoshi-nakamoto">Satoshi Nakamoto</a>, Bitcoin is the largest cryptocurrency measured by market capitalization and amount of data stored on its blockchain. The Bitcoin software is free and available online to anyone who wants to run a Bitcoin node and store their own copy of the Bitcoin blockchain. As Bitcoin matures, engineers have designed additional protocols to improve the speed and privacy of Bitcoin transactions, including the <a href="https://www.omnilayer.org/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Omni Layer</a>, <a href="/learn/bitcoin-101/what-is-the-lightning-network">Lightning Network</a> and Liquid Network. Only approximately 21 million bitcoins will ever be created. New coins are minted every 10 minutes by bitcoin miners who help to maintain the network by adding new transaction data to the blockchain.</p><br />
<p>The Bitcoin price page is part of <a href="/coindesk20">The CoinDesk 20</a> that features price history, price ticker, market cap and live charts for the top cryptocurrencies.</p><br />

2021</span></div></div><p class="card-text">Photo by ojogabonitoo/iStock via Getty Images Thesis Summary Riot Blockchain (RIOT) has been around for a while, but it has only gained such massive As a Bitcoin (BTC-USD) miner, the factors that determine the success and value of this company are the same as</p></div></section><section class="article-card-fh xs dark pre-animation-state"><div
